## ScholarTrack Project Analysis Report

Based on my exploration of the ScholarTrack codebase, here is a comprehensive overview of the data models and services available for building recommendation features:

---

### 1. USER MODEL
**File:** `/e/CourseFile/Year4/Semester 2/Web Services and Web Data/cw1/app/models/user.py`

**Fields:**
- `id` (Integer, Primary Key)
- `username` (String 80, Unique, Indexed)
- `email` (String 120, Unique, Indexed)
- `password_hash` (String 256)
- `preferred_categories` (JSON) - **Key for recommendations**: Stores arXiv category preferences (e.g., ["cs.AI", "cs.LG"])
- `created_at` (DateTime)

**Relationships:**
- `saved_papers` → UserPaper (one-to-many)
- `notes` → Note (one-to-many)
- `tags` → Tag (one-to-many)
- `flashcards` → Flashcard (one-to-many)
- `review_logs` → ReviewLog (one-to-many)

---

### 2. PAPER MODEL
**File:** `/e/CourseFile/Year4/Semester 2/Web Services and Web Data/cw1/app/models/paper.py`

**Paper Fields:**
- `id` (Integer, Primary Key)
- `arxiv_id` (String 50, Unique, Indexed)
- `title` (Text)
- `authors` (Text - stored as JSON array string)
- `abstract` (Text) - **Vector indexed in ChromaDB**
- `categories` (String 200) - arXiv categories space-separated
- `published_date` (Date, Indexed)
- `arxiv_url` (String 300)
- `pdf_url` (String 300)
- `fetched_at` (DateTime)

**Indexed for Vector Search:** Paper abstracts are automatically synced to ChromaDB's `paper_abstracts` collection when fetched.

---

### 3. USER-PAPER RELATIONSHIP
**File:** `/e/CourseFile/Year4/Semester 2/Web Services and Web Data/cw1/app/models/paper.py`

**UserPaper Model** - Represents saved papers with metadata:
- `id` (Integer, Primary Key)
- `user_id` (Foreign Key, Indexed)
- `paper_id` (Foreign Key)
- `memo` (Text) - **User-provided metadata/notes about why they saved it**
- `saved_at` (DateTime) - **Timestamp of save action**
- `tags` (relationship to UserPaperTag) - **User-assigned tags**

**Unique Constraint:** (user_id, paper_id) - Each user can save a paper once

**Tag System:**
- **Tag Model:** user_id, name (unique per user)
- **UserPaperTag Model:** Bridges UserPaper and Tag (many-to-many)
- Tags enable user-defined categorization beyond arXiv categories

---

### 4. CHROMADB SERVICE - VECTOR SEARCH
**File:** `/e/CourseFile/Year4/Semester 2/Web Services and Web Data/cw1/app/services/chromadb_service.py`

**Collections:**
1. **paper_abstracts** - Semantic search over all paper abstracts
   - Vector space: Cosine similarity
   - Documents: Paper abstracts
   - Metadata: arxiv_id, title, categories, published_date

2. **user_notes** - Semantic search over user-created notes
   - Vector space: Cosine similarity
   - Documents: Note content (max 1000 characters per note)
   - Metadata: user_id, paper_id (arxiv_id), created_at

**Available Methods:**
- `search_papers(query, n_results=10)` - Semantic search across all papers
- `search_notes(query, user_id, n_results=10)` - Search user's notes with filtering
- `search_all(query, user_id=None, n_results=10)` - Combined search (papers + notes)
- `add_paper(paper_id, abstract, metadata)` - Index new paper
- `add_note(note_id, content, metadata)` - Index new note

**Returns:**
```python
{
    'ids': [['paper_1', 'paper_2', ...]],
    'distances': [[0.15, 0.25, ...]],  # Cosine distance
    'metadatas': [[{...}, {...}, ...]],
    'documents': [[abstract1, abstract2, ...]]
}
```

---

### 5. ARXIV SERVICE - PAPER DISCOVERY
**File:** `/e/CourseFile/Year4/Semester 2/Web Services and Web Data/cw1/app/services/arxiv_service.py`

**Key Methods:**

**1. Search Papers**
```python
search(query, category=None, date_from=None, date_to=None, 
       max_results=20, offset=0, chromadb_service=None)
```
- Parameters:
  - `query`: Search keywords (or "*" for all)
  - `category`: arXiv category filter (e.g., "cs.AI", "cs.LG")
  - `date_from/date_to`: YYYY-MM-DD format date range
  - `offset`: For pagination
  - `max_results`: Up to 100 per arXiv fairness policy
- Returns: List of Paper objects (cached if already fetched)
- Auto-syncs to ChromaDB

**2. Trending Papers**
```python
trending(category, days=7, max_results=20, offset=0, chromadb_service=None)
```
- Gets recent papers in a category within last N days
- Sorted by submission date (descending)

**3. Fetch by ID**
```python
fetch_by_id(arxiv_id, chromadb_service=None)
```
- Retrieves single paper, returns cached version if available

**Query Building:**
- Supports arXiv query syntax: `cat:{category}`, `all:{query}`, `submittedDate:[...]`
- Date format: YYYYMMDDHHmm (e.g., "202501011200")
- Combines multiple filters with AND

---

### 6. NOTES & LEARNING DATA
**File:** `/e/CourseFile/Year4/Semester 2/Web Services and Web Data/cw1/app/models/note.py`

**Note Model** - User insights linked to papers:
- `id` (Integer, Primary Key)
- `user_id` (Foreign Key, Indexed)
- `paper_id` (Foreign Key)
- `content` (Text, max 1000 chars)
- `created_at` (DateTime)
- `updated_at` (DateTime)

**Relationships:**
- Links to Paper
- Has Flashcards derived from it

---

### 7. FLASHCARD & REVIEW DATA - LEARNING SIGNALS
**File:** `/e/CourseFile/Year4/Semester 2/Web Services and Web Data/cw1/app/models/flashcard.py`

**Flashcard Model** - Spaced repetition cards from notes:
- `id` (Integer)
- `user_id` (Foreign Key, Indexed)
- `note_id` (Foreign Key)
- `question` (Text)
- `answer` (Text)
- `ease_factor` (Float, default 2.5) - **SM-2 algorithm**
- `interval` (Integer, default 1) - **Days until next review**
- `repetitions` (Integer, default 0) - **Number of reviews completed**
- `next_review_at` (DateTime, Indexed) - **Critical for finding due cards**
- `created_at` (DateTime)

**ReviewLog Model** - Detailed review history:
- `id` (Integer)
- `user_id` (Foreign Key, Indexed)
- `flashcard_id` (Foreign Key)
- `rating` (Integer, 0-5) - **0=forgot, 5=perfect recall**
- `reviewed_at` (DateTime)

**Recommendation Signals:**
- Review ratings indicate engagement and interest
- Flashcards created from papers show deeper interest
- High ease_factor indicates mastered concepts
- Review frequency shows learning patterns

---

## KEY DATA AVAILABLE FOR RECOMMENDATIONS

**User Behavior Signals:**
1. **Saved papers** - Papers the user explicitly selected
2. **Paper memos** - User's written context about why they saved papers
3. **User tags** - Custom categories assigned to papers
4. **Preferred categories** - User's stated category preferences
5. **Notes** - User-created insights (up to 1000 chars per note)
6. **Flashcard reviews** - Rating history (0-5 scores, logged with timestamps)
7. **Review frequency** - How actively user reviews material
8. **Ease factors** - Which papers' concepts user found easy/difficult

**Paper Features:**
1. **Abstract** - Available as vector embeddings in ChromaDB
2. **Categories** - Multiple arXiv categories per paper
3. **Authors** - Stored as JSON array
4. **Publication date** - Available for temporal relevance
5. **All cached papers** - Any paper searched/saved is in database with vectors

**Cross-User Data:**
1. **Aggregated paper popularity** - Count of users who saved each paper
2. **Tag frequency** - Which tags are most common (without leaking user identity)
3. **Trending papers** - Based on arXiv trending by category

---

## API ENDPOINTS RELEVANT TO RECOMMENDATIONS

**Discovery:**
- `GET /api/papers/search?q=...&category=...` - Search papers
- `GET /api/papers/trending?category=...&days=7` - Get trending papers
- `POST /api/search/papers` - Semantic search on abstracts

**User Data Access:**
- `GET /api/library` - User's saved papers (with tags, memos)
- `GET /api/notes` - User's notes
- `GET /api/tags` - User's tags with counts
- `GET /api/flashcards` - User's flashcards
- `GET /api/review/stats` - User's review statistics

---

## VECTOR SEARCH CAPABILITIES

**Paper Abstract Search:**
- Query papers by semantic meaning (not just keywords)
- Returns results with cosine distance (0-2 range, normalized to 0-1 relevance)
- No user filtering (global corpus)

**User Note Search:**
- Filter notes by user_id
- Find semantically similar notes to a query
- Identify thematic interests from user's own writings

**Example Use Cases:**
- Find papers similar to ones user has saved
- Identify papers related to user's notes
- Recommend papers matching user's preferred categories
- Cross-reference user interests via semantic similarity

Mix with category-based fresh papers for novelty.\n\n**Proposed endpoints:**\n\n1. `GET /api/recommendations/daily` — personalized daily recommendations\n   - Cold start: fetch recent papers from user's preferred categories via arXiv API\n   - Warm start: 70% ChromaDB similarity-based + 30% category-based fresh papers\n   - Returns ~10 papers, sorted by mix of relevance and recency\n\n2. `GET /api/papers/discover` — random paper discovery\n   - Required param: `category` (arXiv category)\n   - Optional: `days` (default 7, time window)\n   - Fetches a batch from arXiv, returns 3-5 randomly selected papers\n   - Different from trending (which is sorted by date) — this is serendipity\n\n3. `PUT /api/auth/profile` — update user profile (already may exist, need to check)\n   - Must support updating `preferred_categories`\n\n**MCP tools:**\n- `get_daily_recommendations()` — calls recommendation logic\n- `discover_papers(category, days)` — random discovery\n\n### New files needed:\n- app/services/recommendation_service.py — recommendation logic\n- app/routes/recommendations.py — new blueprint\n- tests/test_recommendations.py — tests\n\n### Existing files to modify:\n- app/routes/papers.py — add /api/papers/discover endpoint\n- app/__init__.py — register new blueprint\n- mcp_server.py — add new MCP tools, remove flashcard tools\n- app/routes/auth.py — ensure profile update supports preferred_categories\n\nPlease design a detailed implementation plan with:\n1. ### PHASE 2: Add Daily Recommendations + Random Discovery (new F5)

#### Step 2.1 -- New file: `app/services/recommendation_service.py`

This is the core logic file. The class `RecommendationService` contains two static/class methods:

**`daily_recommendations(user, chromadb_service, arxiv_service_class=ArxivService)`**

Algorithm:
1. Check if user has saved papers: `UserPaper.query.filter_by(user_id=user.id).count()`
2. **Cold start path** (0 saved papers):
   - Read `user.preferred_categories`. If empty, raise `APIError('Set preferred_categories in your profile first.', 400)`.
   - For each category (up to 3), call `ArxivService.trending(category=cat, days=7, max_results=5, chromadb_service=...)`.
   - Merge results, deduplicate by `arxiv_id`, take up to 10 papers.
   - Return list of Paper objects.
3. **Warm start path** (has saved papers):
   - **Similarity-based (70%, ~7 papers):**
     - Fetch user's saved papers: `UserPaper.query.filter_by(user_id=user.id).order_by(UserPaper.saved_at.desc()).limit(10).all()`
     - Pick one at random: `import random; seed_up = random.choice(saved_papers)`
     - Get the seed paper's abstract: `seed_up.paper.abstract`
     - Query ChromaDB: `chromadb_service.search_papers(query=seed_abstract, n_results=20)`
     - From results, filter out papers already saved by the user (check `UserPaper` table).
     - Take top 7.
   - **Category-based freshness (30%, ~3 papers):**
     - Determine categories: use `user.preferred_categories` if set, otherwise extract categories from saved papers (`seed_up.paper.categories.split()`).
     - Pick one category at random.
     - Call `ArxivService.trending(category=cat, days=7, max_results=10, chromadb_service=...)`.
     - Filter out already-saved papers.
     - Take up to 3.
   - Combine similarity + category results, deduplicate by `arxiv_id`.
   - Return up to 10 papers.

**`discover_random(category, days=7, count=5, chromadb_service=None)`**

Algorithm:
1. Validate `category` is provided.
2. Call `ArxivService.trending(category=category, days=days, max_results=20, chromadb_service=chromadb_service)`.
3. From the returned papers, randomly sample `min(count, len(papers))` using `random.sample()`.
4. Return the sampled papers.

Key design decisions for the recommendation algorithm:
- The seed paper for similarity is chosen randomly each call, providing variety across requests.
- Filtering out already-saved papers ensures recommendations are novel.
- The 70/30 split balances relevance with serendipity.
- Falling back to saved paper categories when `preferred_categories` is empty makes the warm path self-sufficient.
- The `discover_random` function is intentionally simple -- it is the "serendipity" endpoint, distinct from trending (which is sorted by date).

#### Step 2.2 -- New file: `app/routes/recommendations.py`

New blueprint: `recommendations_bp = Blueprint('recommendations', __name__, url_prefix='/api')`

**Endpoint 1: `GET /api/recommendations/daily`**
- Decorator: `@jwt_required()`
- Gets user from JWT identity.
- Calls `RecommendationService.daily_recommendations(user, chromadb_service)`.
- Response format:
```json
{
  "data": [
    {
      "arxiv_id": "2401.12345",
      "title": "...",
      "authors": ["..."],
      "abstract": "...",
      "categories": "cs.AI cs.LG",
      "published_date": "2026-04-10",
      "arxiv_url": "...",
      "pdf_url": "...",
      "recommendation_type": "similarity" | "category",
      "_links": {
        "self": "/api/papers/2401.12345",
        "save": "/api/papers/2401.12345/save"
      }
    }
  ],
  "strategy": "warm_start" | "cold_start",
  "count": 10,
  "_links": {
    "self": "/api/recommendations/daily",
    "profile": "/api/users/me"
  }
}
```
- HTTP 200 on success; 400 if cold start and no preferred categories set.

**Endpoint 2: `GET /api/papers/discover`**
- This goes in `app/routes/papers.py` (not the recommendations blueprint), because it is a paper discovery endpoint.
- No auth required (public endpoint, like search and trending).
- Query params: `category` (required), `days` (optional, default 7), `count` (optional, default 5, max 10).
- Calls `RecommendationService.discover_random(category, days, count, chromadb_service)`.
- Response format:
```json
{
  "data": [
    {
      "arxiv_id": "...",
      "title": "...",
      "authors": ["..."],
      "abstract": "...",
      "categories": "...",
      "published_date": "...",
      "_links": {
        "self": "/api/papers/...",
        "save": "/api/papers/.../save"
      }
    }
  ],
  "category": "cs.AI",
  "count": 5,
  "_links": {
    "self": "/api/papers/discover?category=cs.AI&days=7&count=5"
  }
}
```
- HTTP 400 if `category` is missing.

### Implementation Order

2. **Phase 2 Step 2.1** -- `recommendation_service.py` (core logic, no dependencies on routes).

4. **Phase 2 Step 2.2 + 2.3** -- New recommendations blueprint + registration.
5. **Phase 2 Step 2.5** -- MCP server updates.
6. **Phase 2 Step 2.7** -- Tests.
7. **Phase 2 Step 2.8 + Phase 1 Step 1.3** -- All documentation updates last.

### Potential Challenges

1. **ChromaDB query with full abstract as query text**: The `search_papers` method takes a query string. Using a full abstract (~200 words) as the query should work fine with ChromaDB's cosine similarity, but results may be very broad. Consider truncating to first 2-3 sentences if results are poor.

2. **ArxivService.trending network dependency**: The cold start path and category-based portion of warm start require live arXiv API calls. If arXiv is slow or down, recommendations will fail. Consider wrapping in try/except and returning partial results (e.g., only similarity-based papers if arXiv is unreachable).

3. **Deduplication across multiple category fetches**: When fetching from multiple preferred categories in cold start, the same paper may appear in multiple categories. Deduplicate by `arxiv_id` using a dict.

4. **Empty ChromaDB on first use**: If the ChromaDB `paper_abstracts` collection has no documents yet (fresh install), similarity search will return nothing. The warm start path should gracefully fall back to pure category-based recommendations in this case.

## Approved Plan:
# Plan: Replace Flashcards with Recommendations & Random Discovery

## Context

ScholarTrack 定位为"快速刷论文"工具。Flashcard (SM-2) 偏向深度学习/记忆，与定位冲突。替换为每日推荐 + 随机发现，直接服务"发现新论文"的核心体验。

## Phase 1: Remove Flashcards

### Delete files
- `app/models/flashcard.py`
- `app/routes/flashcards.py`
- `app/services/sm2_service.py`
- `tests/test_flashcards.py`

### Clean up references
| File | Remove |
|------|--------|
| `app/models/__init__.py` | Flashcard/ReviewLog import + __all__ entries |
| `app/models/user.py` | `flashcards` and `review_logs` relationships |
| `app/models/note.py` | `flashcards` relationship |
| `app/__init__.py` | flashcards_bp import + register |
| `app/routes/notes.py` | `flashcards` key in _note_response HATEOAS links |
| `mcp_server.py` | Flashcard/ReviewLog/SM2Service imports, `get_due_flashcards` tool, `review_flashcard` tool |

## Phase 2: Add Recommendations (new F5)

### Recommendation algorithm

**Cold start** (no saved papers):
- Require `user.preferred_categories` (已有字段), 未设置则返回 400
- 对每个 category (最多 3 个) 调用 `ArxivService.trending(days=7, max_results=5)`
- 合并去重，返回最多 10 篇

**Warm start** (has saved papers):
- **70% 相似推荐 (~7 篇)**：从用户最近保存的论文中随机选一篇作为 seed，用其 abstract 查询 ChromaDB `search_papers`，过滤已保存论文，不足则多取补位
- **30% 新鲜推荐 (~3 篇)**：从 preferred_categories (或 saved papers 的 categories) 随机选一个 category，调 `ArxivService.trending(days=7)`，过滤已保存
- 合并去重，返回最多 10 篇
- ChromaDB 无结果时 fallback 到纯 category 推荐

**去重策略**:
- 推荐/随机结果中排除用户已保存的论文（查 UserPaper 表），不足时多取补位
- 本地 Paper 表去重由 `ArxivService._paper_from_result()` 已有逻辑处理（按 arxiv_id 查重，存在则返回已有记录）

### New files

**`app/services/recommendation_service.py`**
```
class RecommendationService:
    daily_recommendations(user, chromadb_service) -> (papers, strategy)
    discover_random(category, days, count, chromadb_service) -> papers
```

**`app/routes/recommendations.py`**
```
GET /api/recommendations/daily  [JWT required]
  -> { data: [...papers...], strategy: "cold_start"|"warm_start", count }
```

### Modified files

**`app/routes/papers.py`** — 新增:
```
GET /api/papers/discover?category=cs.AI&days=7&count=5  [public]
  -> { data: [...3-5 random papers...], category, count }
```

**`app/__init__.py`** — 注册 recommendations_bp

**`mcp_server.py`** — 新增:
- `get_daily_recommendations()` — 每日推荐
- `discover_papers(category, days)` — 随机发现

### Tests: `tests/test_recommendations.py`

用 `unittest.mock.patch` mock ArxivService 和 ChromaDB，避免网络调用:
- cold start 无 categories → 400
- cold start 有 categories → 200 + cold_start strategy
- warm start (有 saved papers) → 200 + warm_start strategy
- discover 无 category → 400
- discover 正常 → 200 + 随机子集
- unauthorized → 401

### Existing code to reuse
- `ArxivService.trending()` — `app/services/arxiv_service.py`
- `ChromaDBService.search_papers()` — `app/services/chromadb_service.py`
- `User.preferred_categories` — `app/models/user.py` (JSON field, already exists)
- `PUT /api/users/me` — `app/routes/auth.py:201` (已支持 preferred_categories 更新)
- `_paper_links()` helper — `app/routes/papers.py:13`

## Phase 3: Documentation

更新 CLAUDE.md, README.md 中的 F5 描述、端点数量、MCP 工具列表。 
docs/ 下的规格文档暂不更新（答辩前集中处理）。

## Implementation order

1. Phase 1: 删除 flashcard 代码 + 清理引用
2. `recommendation_service.py` (核心算法)
3. `papers.py` 添加 discover 端点
4. `recommendations.py` + 注册 blueprint
5. `mcp_server.py` 更新
6. Tests
7. Documentation

## Verification

```bash
pytest tests/ -x -q                    # 全部测试通过
pytest tests/test_recommendations.py -v  # 新测试单独验证
```

MCP 验证: 用 `mcp__scholartrack__get_daily_recommendations` 和 `mcp__scholartrack__discover_papers` 工具实测

1	"""ScholarTrack MCP Server — exposes core API functionality as tools for AI assistants.
2	
3	Calls the service/database layer directly (not via HTTP).
4	Configure in Claude Desktop or Claude Code as a local MCP server.
5	
6	Usage:
7	    python mcp_server.py [--user-id USER_ID]
8	"""
9	import argparse
10	import json
11	import sys
12	from datetime import date, datetime, timedelta
13	
14	from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP

18	from app.models.user import User
19	from app.models.paper import Paper, UserPaper

32	def _get_app():
33	    global _app
34	    if _app is None:
35	        _app = create_app('development')
36	    return _app

39	def _chromadb():
40	    return _get_app().extensions.get('chromadb')

43	@mcp.tool()
44	def search_papers(query: str, category: str = None, days: int = 30) -> str:
45	    """Search arXiv for papers by keyword and optional category.
46	
47	    Args:
48	        query: Search keywords (e.g. "vision transformer").
49	        category: arXiv category filter (e.g. "cs.CV"). Optional.
50	        days: Only return papers from the last N days. Default 30.
51	    """
52	    with _get_app().app_context():
53	        date_from = (date.today() - timedelta(days=days)).isoformat()
54	        date_to = date.today().isoformat()
55	        papers = ArxivService.search(
56	            query=query,
57	            category=category,
58	            date_from=date_from,
59	            date_to=date_to,
60	            max_results=10,
61	            chromadb_service=_chromadb(),
62	        )
63	        results = [p.to_dict() for p in papers]
64	        return json.dumps(results, indent=2)
65

67	@mcp.tool()
68	def get_trending_papers(category: str, days: int = 7) -> str:
69	    """Get recent trending papers in a specific arXiv category.
70	
71	    Args:
72	        category: arXiv category (e.g. "cs.CV", "cs.CL", "cs.AI").
73	        days: Number of days to look back. Default 7.
74	    """
75	    with _get_app().app_context():
76	        papers = ArxivService.trending(
77	            category=category,
78	            days=days,
79	            max_results=10,
80	            chromadb_service=_chromadb(),
81	        )
82	        results = [p.to_dict() for p in papers]
83	        return json.dumps(results, indent=2)

86	@mcp.tool()
87	def save_paper(arxiv_id: str, memo: str = None) -> str:
88	    """Save a paper to the user's personal library.
89	
90	    Args:
91	        arxiv_id: The arXiv paper ID (e.g. "2401.12345").
92	        memo: Optional personal note about why you're saving this paper.
93	    """
94	    with _get_app().app_context():
95	        paper = ArxivService.fetch_by_id(arxiv_id, chromadb_service=_chromadb())
96	        if not paper:
97	            return json.dumps({'error': f'Paper {arxiv_id} not found on arXiv.'})
98	
99	        existing = UserPaper.query.filter_by(user_id=_user_id, paper_id=paper.id).first()
100	        if existing:
101	            return json.dumps({'message': 'Paper already saved.', 'arxiv_id': arxiv_id})
102	
103	        up = UserPaper(user_id=_user_id, paper_id=paper.id, memo=memo)
104	        db.session.add(up)
105	        db.session.commit()
106	        return json.dumps({'message': 'Paper saved.', 'arxiv_id': arxiv_id, 'title': paper.title})

109	@mcp.tool()
110	def list_library() -> str:
111	    """List all papers in the user's personal library."""
112	    with _get_app().app_context():
113	        user_papers = UserPaper.query.filter_by(user_id=_user_id).order_by(
114	            UserPaper.saved_at.desc()
115	        ).limit(20).all()
116	
117	        results = []
118	        for up in user_papers:
119	            results.append({
120	                'arxiv_id': up.paper.arxiv_id,
121	                'title': up.paper.title,
122	                'memo': up.memo,
123	                'tags': [upt.tag.name for upt in up.tags],
124	                'saved_at': up.saved_at.isoformat(),
125	            })
126	        return json.dumps(results, indent=2)

129	@mcp.tool()
130	def create_note(arxiv_id: str, content: str) -> str:
131	    """Create a short insight note linked to a paper (max 1000 characters).
132	
133	    Args:
134	        arxiv_id: arXiv paper ID to link the note to (required).
135	        content: Insight content (max 1000 characters).
136	    """
137	    with _get_app().app_context():
138	        from app.models.note import NOTE_MAX_LENGTH
139	        if len(content) > NOTE_MAX_LENGTH:
140	            return json.dumps({'error': f'Content exceeds {NOTE_MAX_LENGTH} characters.'})
141	
142	        paper = Paper.query.filter_by(arxiv_id=arxiv_id).first()
143	        if not paper:
144	            return json.dumps({'error': f'Paper {arxiv_id} not found.'})
145	
146	        note = Note(user_id=_user_id, paper_id=paper.id, content=content)
147	        db.session.add(note)
148	        db.session.commit()
149	
150	        # Sync to ChromaDB
151	        service = _chromadb()
152	        if service:
153	            try:
154	                service.add_note(
155	                    note_id=note.id,
156	                    content=content,
157	                    metadata={
158	                        'user_id': _user_id,
159	                        'paper_id': arxiv_id,
160	                        'created_at': note.created_at.isoformat(),
161	                    },
162	                )
163	            except Exception:
164	                pass
165	
166	        return json.dumps({
167	            'message': 'Note created.',
168	            'id': note.id,
169	            'arxiv_id': arxiv_id,
170	            'preview': content[:100],
171	        })

174	@mcp.tool()
175	def search_notes(query: str) -> str:
176	    """Semantic search across your personal research notes.
177	
178	    Args:
179	        query: Natural language search query.
180	    """
181	    with _get_app().app_context():
182	        service = _chromadb()
183	        if not service:
184	            return json.dumps([])
185	
186	        try:
187	            results = service.search_notes(query, user_id=_user_id, n_results=5)
188	        except Exception:
189	            return json.dumps([])
190	
191	        items = []
192	        if results and results.get('ids') and results['ids'][0]:
193	            for doc_id, distance in zip(results['ids'][0], results['distances'][0]):
194	                try:
195	                    note_id = int(doc_id.replace('note_', ''))
196	                    note = db.session.get(Note, note_id)
197	                    if note:
198	                        items.append({
199	                            'id': note.id,
200	                            'preview': note.content[:100],
201	                            'arxiv_id': note.paper.arxiv_id if note.paper else None,
202	                            'relevance_score': round(max(0, 1 - distance), 4),
203	                        })
204	                except (ValueError, AttributeError):
205	                    continue
206	        return json.dumps(items, indent=2)
207	
208	
209	@mcp.tool()
210	def search_knowledge(query: str) -> str:
211	    """Search across both papers and personal notes for relevant knowledge.
212	
213	    Args:
214	        query: Natural language search query.
215	    """
216	    with _get_app().app_context():
217	        service = _chromadb()
218	        if not service:
219	            return json.dumps([])
220	
221	        try:
222	            combined = service.search_all(query, user_id=_user_id, n_results=5)
223	        except Exception:
224	            return json.dumps([])
225	
226	        items = []
227	        # Process papers
228	        paper_results = combined.get('papers')
229	        if paper_results and paper_results.get('ids') and paper_results['ids'][0]:
230	            for doc_id, distance, meta in zip(
231	                paper_results['ids'][0],
232	                paper_results['distances'][0],
233	                paper_results['metadatas'][0],
234	            ):
235	                items.append({
236	                    'type': 'paper',
237	                    'arxiv_id': meta.get('arxiv_id', ''),
238	                    'title': meta.get('title', ''),
239	                    'relevance_score': round(max(0, 1 - distance), 4),
240	                })
241	
242	        # Process notes
243	        note_results = combined.get('notes')
244	        if note_results and note_results.get('ids') and note_results['ids'][0]:
245	            for doc_id, distance in zip(note_results['ids'][0], note_results['distances'][0]):
246	                try:
247	                    note_id = int(doc_id.replace('note_', ''))
248	                    note = db.session.get(Note, note_id)
249	                    if note:
250	                        items.append({
251	                            'type': 'note',
252	                            'id': note.id,
253	                            'preview': note.content[:100],
254	                            'arxiv_id': note.paper.arxiv_id if note.paper else None,
255	                            'relevance_score': round(max(0, 1 - distance), 4),
256	                        })
257	                except (ValueError, AttributeError):
258	                    continue
259	
260	        items.sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)
261	        return json.dumps(items, indent=2)
262	
263	
264	@mcp.tool()
265	def get_due_flashcards() -> str:
266	    """Get flashcards that are due for review today."""
267	    with _get_app().app_context():
268	        now = datetime.utcnow()
269	        cards = Flashcard.query.filter(
270	            Flashcard.user_id == _user_id,
271	            Flashcard.next_review_at <= now,
272	        ).order_by(Flashcard.next_review_at.asc()).limit(20).all()
273	
274	        results = []
275	        for card in cards:
276	            results.append({
277	                'id': card.id,
278	                'question': card.question,
279	                'answer': card.answer,
280	                'ease_factor': card.ease_factor,
281	                'interval': card.interval,
282	            })
283	        return json.dumps(results, indent=2)

285	
286	@mcp.tool()
287	def review_flashcard(flashcard_id: int, rating: int) -> str:
288	    """Submit a review rating for a flashcard (SM-2 spaced repetition).
289	
290	    Args:
291	        flashcard_id: The ID of the flashcard to review.
292	        rating: Score from 0-5 (0=forgot completely, 5=perfect recall).
293	    """
294	    with _get_app().app_context():
295	        card = db.session.get(Flashcard, flashcard_id)
296	        if not card or card.user_id != _user_id:
297	            return json.dumps({'error': 'Flashcard not found.'})
298	
299	        if rating < 0 or rating > 5:
300	            return json.dumps({'error': 'Rating must be 0-5.'})
301	
302	        updated = SM2Service.review(card, rating)
303	        card.ease_factor = updated['ease_factor']
304	        card.interval = updated['interval']
305	        card.repetitions = updated['repetitions']
306	        card.next_review_at = updated['next_review_at']
307	
308	        log = ReviewLog(user_id=_user_id, flashcard_id=card.id, rating=rating)
309	        db.session.add(log)
310	        db.session.commit()
311	
312	        return json.dumps({
313	            'message': 'Review recorded.',
314	            'next_review_at': card.next_review_at.isoformat(),
315	            'interval': card.interval,
316	            'ease_factor': card.ease_factor,
317	        })
318

321	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='ScholarTrack MCP Server')
322	    parser.add_argument('--user-id', type=int, default=1, help='Default user ID')
323	    args = parser.parse_args()
324	    _user_id = args.user_id
325	    mcp.run()

if saved_count == 0:\n            return cls._cold_start(user, chromadb_service)\n        else:\n            return cls._warm_start(user, chromadb_service)\n\n    @classmethod\n    def _cold_start(cls, user, chromadb_service):\n        \"\"\"Recommend based on preferred categories only.\"\"\"\n        categories = user.preferred_categories or []\n        if not categories:\n            from app.utils.errors import APIError\n            raise APIError(\n                'Set preferred_categories in your profile first '\n                '(PUT /api/users/me).',\n                400,\n            )\n\n        saved_ids = cls._get_saved_arxiv_ids(user.id)\n        seen = set()\n        papers = []\n\n        for cat in categories[:3]:\n            try:\n                batch = ArxivService.trending(\n                    category=cat,\n                    days=7,\n                    max_results=10,\n                    chromadb_service=chromadb_service,\n                )\n                for p in batch:\n                    if p.arxiv_id not in seen and p.arxiv_id not in saved_ids:\n                        seen.add(p.arxiv_id)\n                        papers.append(p)\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning('Cold start trending fetch failed for %s: %s', cat, e)\n\n        return papers[:cls.TOTAL_TARGET], 'cold_start'\n\n    @classmethod\n    def _warm_start(cls, user, chromadb_service):\n        \"\"\"Recommend via similarity + fresh category papers.\"\"\"\n        saved_ids = cls._get_saved_arxiv_ids(user.id)\n        seen = set(saved_ids)\n        papers = []\n\n        # --- Similarity-based portion ---\n        sim_papers = cls._similarity_recommendations(\n            user, chromadb_service, saved_ids, seen,\n        )\n        papers.extend(sim_papers)\n\n        # --- Category-based freshness portion ---\n        cat_papers = cls._category_recommendations(\n            user, chromadb_service, seen,\n        )\n        papers.extend(cat_papers)\n\n        return papers[:cls.TOTAL_TARGET], 'warm_start'\n\n    @classmethod\n    def _similarity_recommendations(cls, user, chromadb_service, saved_ids, seen):\n        \"\"\"Find papers similar to user's saved papers via ChromaDB.\"\"\"\n        if not chromadb_service:\n            return []\n\n        recent_saved = (\n            UserPaper.query\n            .filter_by(user_id=user.id)\n            .order_by(UserPaper.saved_at.desc())\n            .limit(10)\n            .all()\n        )\n        if not recent_saved:\n            return []\n\n        seed = random.choice(recent_saved)\n        query_text = seed.paper.abstract\n        if not query_text:\n            return []\n\n        try:\n            # Fetch extra results to allow filtering\n            results = chromadb_service.search_papers(\n                query=query_text,\n                n_results=30,\n            )\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning('ChromaDB similarity search failed: %s', e)\n            return []\n\n        papers = []\n        if results and results.get('ids') and results['ids'][0]:\n            metadatas = results.get('metadatas', [[]])[0]\n            for meta in metadatas:\n                arxiv_id = meta.get('arxiv_id', '')\n                if arxiv_id and arxiv_id not in seen:\n                    paper = Paper.query.filter_by(arxiv_id=arxiv_id).first()\n                    if paper:\n                        seen.add(arxiv_id)\n                        papers.append(paper)\n                        if len(papers) >= cls.SIMILARITY_COUNT:\n                            break\n\n        return papers\n\n    @classmethod\n    def _category_recommendations(cls, user, chromadb_service, seen):\n        \"\"\"Fetch fresh papers from a preferred or inferred category.\"\"\"\n        categories = user.preferred_categories or []\n\n        # Fallback: infer categories from saved papers\n        if not categories:\n            recent = (\n                UserPaper.query\n                .filter_by(user_id=user.id)\n                .order_by(UserPaper.saved_at.desc())\n                .limit(5)\n                .all()\n            )\n            for up in recent:\n                if up.paper.categories:\n                    categories.extend(up.paper.categories.split())\n            categories = list(set(categories))\n\n        if not categories:\n            return []\n\n        cat = random.choice(categories)\n        papers = []\n        try:\n            batch = ArxivService.trending(\n                category=cat,\n                days=7,\n                max_results=15,\n                chromadb_service=chromadb_service,\n            )\n            for p in batch:\n                if p.arxiv_id not in seen:\n                    seen.add(p.arxiv_id)\n                    papers.append(p)\n                    if len(papers) >= cls.CATEGORY_COUNT:\n                        break\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning('Category trending fetch failed for %s: %s', cat, e)\n\n        return papers\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _get_saved_arxiv_ids(user_id):\n        \"\"\"Return a set of arxiv_ids for papers saved by the user.\"\"\"\n        rows = (\n            db.session.query(Paper.arxiv_id)\n            .join(UserPaper, UserPaper.paper_id == Paper.id)\n            .filter(UserPaper.user_id == user_id)\n            .all()\n        )\n        return {r[0] for r in rows}\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def discover_random(category, days=7, count=5, chromadb_service=None):\n        \"\"\"Return a random subset of recent papers in a category.\"\"\"\n        papers = ArxivService.trending(\n            category=category,\n            days=days,\n            max_results=max(count * 4, 20),\n            chromadb_service=chromadb_service,\n        )\n        if len(papers) <= count:\n            return papers\n        return random.sample(papers, count)\n"
}

1	# CLAUDE.md
2	
3	This file provides guidance to Claude Code (claude.ai/code) when working with code in this repository.
4	
5	## Project Overview
6	
7	**ScholarTrack** — a RESTful Web API for researchers to track arXiv papers, manage research notes, and use spaced repetition learning. University coursework (XJCO3011) due April 21, 2026, with oral examination April 28–May 7.
8	
9	## Tech Stack
10	
11	- **Framework:** Flask 3.1.1 with app factory pattern
12	- **Database:** SQLite + SQLAlchemy 2.0 ORM
13	- **Auth:** JWT via flask-jwt-extended
14	- **Vector Search:** ChromaDB (RAG semantic search over papers/notes)
15	- **External API:** arXiv Python client for paper discovery
16	- **Validation:** Marshmallow
17	- **Docs:** Flasgger (Swagger/OpenAPI)
18	- **MCP:** mcp SDK for AI assistant tool integration
19	- **Testing:** pytest + pytest-cov
20	
21	## Commands
22	
23	```bash
24	pip install -r requirements.txt      # Install dependencies
25	python run.py                        # Start Flask dev server (port 5000)
26	pytest                               # Run all tests
27	pytest --cov=app tests/              # Run tests with coverage
28	pytest tests/test_auth.py            # Run single test module
29	pytest tests/test_auth.py::test_name -v  # Run single test
30	```
31	
32	Swagger UI available at `http://localhost:5000/apidocs` when server is running.
33	
34	## Architecture
35	
36	```
37	app/
38	├── __init__.py          # Flask app factory (create_app)
39	├── config.py            # Dev/test/prod configuration
40	├── models/              # SQLAlchemy models (8 tables)
41	├── routes/              # Flask Blueprints (API endpoints)
42	│   ├── auth.py          # F1: register, login, profile
43	│   ├── papers.py        # F2+F3: arXiv search, collections, tags
44	│   ├── notes.py         # F4: research notes CRUD
45	│   ├── flashcards.py    # F5: spaced repetition (SM-2)
46	│   └── search.py        # F6: RAG semantic search
47	├── services/            # Business logic
48	│   ├── arxiv_service.py    # arXiv API wrapper with caching
49	│   ├── chromadb_service.py # Vector DB operations
50	│   └── sm2_service.py      # SM-2 spaced repetition algorithm
51	└── utils/               # Error handling, pagination, validation
52	mcp_server.py            # MCP server entry (calls services directly, not HTTP)
53	```
54	
55	**Data flow:** arXiv API → Paper table (cached) + ChromaDB `paper_abstracts` collection. User notes sync to ChromaDB `user_notes` collection. Notes are user-isolated via metadata filtering.
56	
57	**30 endpoints** across 7 feature modules (F1–F7). All authenticated endpoints require JWT. Responses follow HATEOAS with `_links` and standard error format.
58	
59	## Key Design Decisions
60	
61	- **Papers are read-only from arXiv** — no user uploads. Papers cached in SQLite on first fetch, abstracts indexed in ChromaDB.
62	- **UserPaper** is the many-to-many join between users and papers (collections). Tags attach to UserPaper, not Paper directly.
63	- **ChromaDB** uses built-in `all-MiniLM-L6-v2` embeddings (no external model deployment).
64	- **MCP server** calls the service layer directly (not via HTTP routes).
65	- **SM-2 algorithm:** ease_factor min 1.3, rating < 3 resets interval to 1, rating >= 3 multiplies interval by ease_factor.
66	
67	## Specification Documents
68	
69	All design specs are in `docs/`. Key references:
70	- `04-feature_spec.md` — detailed feature requirements per module
71	- `05-data_models.md` — SQLAlchemy models and ChromaDB collections schema
72	- `06-api_spec.md` — complete endpoint spec with request/response examples
73	
74	## Development Environment
75	
76	- **Conda env:** `scholartrack` (all dependencies pre-installed)
77	- Run commands with: `D:/anaconda3/envs/scholartrack/python.exe` or `conda run -n scholartrack` (note: `conda run` does not support multi-line arguments)
78	- `conda run` may hit GBK encoding issues on Windows; prefer setting `PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8` or using the Python path directly
79	- **Language:** All code, comments, commit messages, and documentation must be in English
80	
81	## Agent Workflow
82	
83	- **Max 2 concurrent agents** to avoid performance issues
84	- **Team Lead (main process) coordinates** — splits tasks, sets dependencies, monitors progress, resolves conflicts
85	- **Developer agent** for large independent code blocks (e.g., implementing an entire feature module)
86	- **Reviewer agent** for milestone reviews and quality checks
87	- **Team Lead implements directly** for small fixes, bug patches, and when agent idle latency outweighs parallelism benefits
88	- When an agent is slow to respond, Team Lead takes over rather than waiting
89	
90	## Git Conventions
91	
92	Commit format: `feat(module): description`, `fix(module):`, `docs:`, `test:`
93	
94	Do not commit: `*.db`, `.env`, `__pycache__/`, `chroma_data/`, `*.pyc`
95

Claudeclaude-opus-4-62026-04-14 19:49:05





这是 ChromaDB 的遥测(telemetry)模块和当前安装的某个依赖版本不兼容导致的警告。capture() 方法签名变了，ChromaDB 内部尝试发送使用统计时失败。




对功能没有任何影响——遥测只是 ChromaDB 用来收集匿名使用数据的，失败了就是不发送而已，不影响向量搜索和存储。




如果觉得日志刺眼，可以关掉 ChromaDB 遥测：

Claudeclaude-opus-4-62026-04-14 19:53:08
总结：这是 ChromaDB 1.0.7 内部的 posthog 兼容性 bug，它在创建 client 实例时尝试发遥测数据但 capture() 方法签名与当前 posthog 版本不匹配。对功能完全无影响——遥测发送失败就是不发送，向量搜索和存储都正常工作。这个警告只出现在 stderr，不影响 API 响应、测试结果、MCP 调用。

Tool result: toolu_019z8qAvUCeBtfw1zHEDfmBr
1	# ScholarTrack
2	
3	A RESTful Web API for researchers to track arXiv papers, manage research notes, and use spaced repetition learning. Built with Flask for the XJCO3011 Web Services and Web Data coursework.
4	
5	## Features
6	
7	- **Paper Discovery (F2)** — Search and browse arXiv papers with category filtering
8	- **Paper Management (F3)** — Save papers to a personal library with tags and memos
9	- **Research Notes (F4)** — Full CRUD note-taking linked to papers, with Markdown support
10	- **Flashcards & SM-2 (F5)** — Spaced repetition flashcards using the SM-2 algorithm
11	- **RAG Semantic Search (F6)** — Vector search over paper abstracts and notes via ChromaDB
12	- **MCP Server (F7)** — AI assistant integration through the Model Context Protocol
13	
14	## Tech Stack
15	
16	| Component | Technology |
17	|-----------|-----------|
18	| Framework | Flask 3.1.1 |
19	| Database | SQLite + SQLAlchemy 2.0 |
20	| Authentication | JWT (flask-jwt-extended) |
21	| Vector Search | ChromaDB 1.0.7 |
22	| External API | arXiv Python client |
23	| API Documentation | Flasgger (Swagger/OpenAPI) |
24	| Testing | pytest + pytest-cov |
25	
26	## Quick Start
27	
28	### Prerequisites
29	
30	- Python 3.11+
31	- pip or conda
32	
33	### Installation
34	
35	```bash
36	# Clone the repository
37	git clone https://github.com/Nuo-cl/ScholarTrack.git
38	cd ScholarTrack
39	
40	# Create and activate a virtual environment (or use conda)
41	python -m venv venv
42	source venv/bin/activate  # On Windows: venv\Scripts\activate
43	
44	# Install dependencies
45	pip install -r requirements.txt
46	```
47	
48	### Running the Server
49	
50	```bash
51	python run.py
52	```
53	
54	The API server starts at `http://localhost:5000`. Swagger UI is available at `http://localhost:5000/apidocs`.
55	
56	### Running Tests
57	
58	```bash
59	# Run all tests
60	pytest
61	
62	# Run with coverage report
63	pytest --cov=app tests/
64	
65	# Run a specific test module
66	pytest tests/test_auth.py -v
67	```
68	
69	## API Overview
70	
71	**30 endpoints** across 7 feature modules. Base URL: `/api`
72	
73	| Module | Endpoints | Auth Required |
74	|--------|-----------|---------------|
75	| Authentication (F1) | 4 | Partial |
76	| Paper Discovery (F2) | 3 | No |
77	| Paper Management (F3) | 6 | Yes |
78	| Notes (F4) | 6 | Yes |
79	| Flashcards (F5) | 5 | Yes |
80	| Spaced Repetition (F5) | 3 | Yes |
81	| Semantic Search (F6) | 3 | Partial |
82	
83	Full API documentation is available in [`docs/api_documentation.pdf`](docs/api_documentation.pdf).
84	Interactive Swagger UI is at `/apidocs` when the server is running.
85	
86	### Authentication
87	
88	All authenticated endpoints require a JWT bearer token in the `Authorization` header:
89	
90	```
91	Authorization: Bearer <access_token>
92	```
93	
94	Tokens expire after 24 hours.
95	
96	### Common API Usage Examples
97	
98	**Register a new account:**
99	
100	```bash
101	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/register \
102	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
103	  -d '{"username": "researcher1", "email": "researcher1@example.com", "password": "securepass123"}'
104	```
105	
106	**Login and obtain a token:**
107	
108	```bash
109	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/login \
110	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
111	  -d '{"username": "researcher1", "password": "securepass123"}'
112	```
113	
114	Response:
115	
116	```json
117	{
118	  "data": {
119	    "access_token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIs...",
120	    "token_type": "bearer",
121	    "expires_in": 86400
122	  }
123	}
124	```
125	
126	**Search arXiv papers (no auth required):**
127	
128	```bash
129	curl "http://localhost:5000/api/papers/search?q=vision+transformer&category=cs.CV"
130	```
131	
132	**Save a paper to your library:**
133	
134	```bash
135	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/papers/2403.12345/save \
136	  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
137	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
138	  -d '{"memo": "Interesting attention approach"}'
139	```
140	
141	**Create a research note linked to a paper:**
142	
143	```bash
144	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/notes \
145	  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
146	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
147	  -d '{"paper_id": "2403.12345", "title": "Key Ideas", "content": "## Summary\n\nNovel multi-scale attention mechanism..."}'
148	```
149	
150	**Create a flashcard from a note:**
151	
152	```bash
153	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/flashcards \
154	  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
155	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
156	  -d '{"note_id": 1, "question": "What is Multi-Head Attention?", "answer": "A mechanism that runs multiple attention functions in parallel."}'
157	```
158	
159	**Review a flashcard (SM-2 spaced repetition):**
160	
161	```bash
162	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/flashcards/1/review \
163	  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
164	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
165	  -d '{"rating": 4}'
166	```
167	
168	Rating scale: 0 (forgot completely) to 5 (perfect recall). The SM-2 algorithm adjusts the review interval accordingly.
169	
170	**Semantic search across papers and notes:**
171	
172	```bash
173	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/search/all \
174	  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
175	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
176	  -d '{"query": "attention mechanism improvements", "n_results": 10}'
177	```
178	
179	For the complete list of all 30 endpoints with request/response examples, see the [API Documentation](docs/api_documentation.pdf).
180	
181	## MCP Server
182	
183	ScholarTrack includes an MCP (Model Context Protocol) server that exposes core functionality as tools for AI assistants such as Claude. The MCP server calls the service layer directly (not via HTTP), so the Flask web server does not need to be running.
184	
185	### Available Tools
186	
187	| Tool | Description |
188	|------|-------------|
189	| `search_papers` | Search arXiv for papers by keyword and optional category |
190	| `get_trending_papers` | Get recent trending papers in an arXiv category |
191	| `save_paper` | Save a paper to the user's personal library |
192	| `list_library` | List all papers in the user's library |
193	| `create_note` | Create a research note, optionally linked to a paper |
194	| `search_notes` | Semantic search across personal research notes |
195	| `search_knowledge` | Search across both papers and notes |
196	| `get_due_flashcards` | Get flashcards due for review today |
197	| `review_flashcard` | Submit a review rating for a flashcard (SM-2) |
198	
199	### Running Standalone
200	
201	```bash
202	python mcp_server.py [--user-id USER_ID]
203	```
204	
205	The `--user-id` flag specifies which user's data to operate on (default: 1). The MCP server bypasses JWT authentication and accesses the database directly.
206	
207	### Configuring with Claude Code
208	
209	Create a `.mcp.json` file in the project root:
210	
211	```json
212	{
213	  "mcpServers": {
214	    "scholartrack": {
215	      "command": "python",
216	      "args": ["mcp_server.py", "--user-id", "1"],
217	      "cwd": "/path/to/ScholarTrack"
218	    }
219	  }
220	}
221	```
222	
223	After restarting Claude Code, the AI assistant can directly invoke tools like `search_papers`, `save_paper`, `create_note`, etc. For example, you can ask Claude to "search for recent papers on vision transformers" and it will call the `search_papers` tool automatically.
224	
225	### Configuring with Claude Desktop
226	
227	Add the following to your Claude Desktop MCP settings (`claude_desktop_config.json`):
228	
229	```json
230	{
231	  "mcpServers": {
232	    "scholartrack": {
233	      "command": "python",
234	      "args": ["mcp_server.py", "--user-id", "1"],
235	      "cwd": "/path/to/ScholarTrack"
236	    }
237	  }
238	}
239	```
240	
241	## Project Structure
242	
243	```
244	app/
245	├── __init__.py          # Flask app factory
246	├── config.py            # Configuration (dev/test/prod)
247	├── models/              # SQLAlchemy models (8 tables)
248	├── routes/              # API endpoints (5 Blueprint modules)
249	├── services/            # Business logic (arXiv, ChromaDB, SM-2)
250	└── utils/               # Error handling, pagination, validation
251	tests/                   # pytest test suite (66 tests)
252	docs/                    # Design specs and API documentation
253	mcp_server.py            # MCP server for AI assistants
254	```
255	
256	## License
257	
258	This project is coursework for XJCO3011 at the University of Leeds.
259

Detailed API documentation is available in [`docs/api_documentation.pdf`](docs/api_documentation.pdf).\n\n### Quick Example\n\n```bash\n# Register and login\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/register \\\n  -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n  -d '{\"username\": \"researcher1\", \"email\": \"r1@example.com\", \"password\": \"securepass123\"}'\n\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/login \\\n  -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n  -d '{\"username\": \"researcher1\", \"password\": \"securepass123\"}'\n# -> returns { \"data\": { \"access_token\": \"eyJ...\" } }\n\n# Search papers (no auth required)\ncurl \"http://localhost:5000/api/papers/search?q=vision+transformer&category=cs.CV\"\n\n# Get daily recommendations (auth required)\ncurl http://localhost:5000/api/recommendations/daily \\\n  -H \"Authorization: Bearer <token>\"\n```\n\n## Project Structure\n\n```\napp/\n├── __init__.py          # Flask app factory\n├── config.py            # Configuration (dev/test/prod)\n├── models/              # SQLAlchemy models (6 tables)\n├── routes/              # API endpoints (5 Blueprint modules)\n├── services/            # Business logic (arXiv, ChromaDB, recommendations)\n└── utils/               # Error handling, pagination, validation\ntests/                   # pytest test suite\ndocs/                    # Design specs and API documentation\nmcp_server.py            # MCP server for AI assistants\n```\n\n## License\n\nThis project is coursework for XJCO3011 at the University of Leeds.\n"

     ```python
     def search(cls, query, category=None, datefrom=None, dateto=None,


                maxresults=20, offset=0, chromadbservice=None):


         searchquery = cls.buildquery(query, category, datefrom, date_to)


         fetchcount = min(offset + maxresults, cls.MAXARXIVFETCH)


         search = arxiv.Search(query=searchquery, maxresults=fetch_count, ...)


         papers = []


         for result in islice(cls.client.results(search), offset, offset + maxresults):


             paper = cls.paperfrom_result(result)


             papers.append(paper)


     ```

1	import logging
2	import random
3	
4	from app import db
5	from app.models.paper import Paper, UserPaper
6	from app.services.arxiv_service import ArxivService
7	
8	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
9	
10	
11	class RecommendationService:
12	    """Personalized paper recommendations and random discovery."""
13	
14	    # Target counts for warm-start mixing strategy
15	    SIMILARITY_COUNT = 7
16	    CATEGORY_COUNT = 3
17	    TOTAL_TARGET = 10
18	
19	    @classmethod
20	    def daily_recommendations(cls, user, chromadb_service=None):
21	        """Generate daily paper recommendations for a user.
22	
23	        Returns:
24	            Tuple of (list[Paper], strategy_name).
25	        """
26	        saved_count = UserPaper.query.filter_by(user_id=user.id).count()
27	
28	        if saved_count == 0:
29	            return cls._cold_start(user, chromadb_service)
30	        else:
31	            return cls._warm_start(user, chromadb_service)
32	
33	    @classmethod
34	    def _cold_start(cls, user, chromadb_service):
35	        """Recommend based on preferred categories only."""
36	        categories = user.preferred_categories or []
37	        if not categories:
38	            from app.utils.errors import APIError
39	            raise APIError(
40	                'Set preferred_categories in your profile first '
41	                '(PUT /api/users/me).',
42	                400,
43	            )
44	
45	        saved_ids = cls._get_saved_arxiv_ids(user.id)
46	        seen = set()
47	        papers = []
48	
49	        for cat in categories[:3]:
50	            try:
51	                batch = ArxivService.trending(
52	                    category=cat,
53	                    days=7,
54	                    max_results=10,
55	                    chromadb_service=chromadb_service,
56	                )
57	                for p in batch:
58	                    if p.arxiv_id not in seen and p.arxiv_id not in saved_ids:
59	                        seen.add(p.arxiv_id)
60	                        papers.append(p)
61	            except Exception as e:
62	                logger.warning('Cold start trending fetch failed for %s: %s', cat, e)
63	
64	        return papers[:cls.TOTAL_TARGET], 'cold_start'
65	
66	    @classmethod
67	    def _warm_start(cls, user, chromadb_service):
68	        """Recommend via similarity + fresh category papers."""
69	        saved_ids = cls._get_saved_arxiv_ids(user.id)
70	        seen = set(saved_ids)
71	        papers = []
72	
73	        # --- Similarity-based portion ---
74	        sim_papers = cls._similarity_recommendations(
75	            user, chromadb_service, saved_ids, seen,
76	        )
77	        papers.extend(sim_papers)
78	
79	        # --- Category-based freshness portion ---
80	        cat_papers = cls._category_recommendations(
81	            user, chromadb_service, seen,
82	        )
83	        papers.extend(cat_papers)
84	
85	        return papers[:cls.TOTAL_TARGET], 'warm_start'
86	
87	    @classmethod
88	    def _similarity_recommendations(cls, user, chromadb_service, saved_ids, seen):
89	        """Find papers similar to user's saved papers via ChromaDB."""
90	        if not chromadb_service:
91	            return []
92	
93	        recent_saved = (
94	            UserPaper.query
95	            .filter_by(user_id=user.id)
96	            .order_by(UserPaper.saved_at.desc())
97	            .limit(10)
98	            .all()
99	        )
100	        if not recent_saved:
101	            return []
102	
103	        seed = random.choice(recent_saved)
104	        query_text = seed.paper.abstract
105	        if not query_text:
106	            return []
107	
108	        try:
109	            # Fetch extra results to allow filtering
110	            results = chromadb_service.search_papers(
111	                query=query_text,
112	                n_results=30,
113	            )
114	        except Exception as e:
115	            logger.warning('ChromaDB similarity search failed: %s', e)
116	            return []
117	
118	        papers = []
119	        if results and results.get('ids') and results['ids'][0]:
120	            metadatas = results.get('metadatas', [[]])[0]
121	            for meta in metadatas:
122	                arxiv_id = meta.get('arxiv_id', '')
123	                if arxiv_id and arxiv_id not in seen:
124	                    paper = Paper.query.filter_by(arxiv_id=arxiv_id).first()
125	                    if paper:
126	                        seen.add(arxiv_id)
127	                        papers.append(paper)
128	                        if len(papers) >= cls.SIMILARITY_COUNT:
129	                            break
130	
131	        return papers
132	
133	    @classmethod
134	    def _category_recommendations(cls, user, chromadb_service, seen):
135	        """Fetch fresh papers from a preferred or inferred category."""
136	        categories = user.preferred_categories or []
137	
138	        # Fallback: infer categories from saved papers
139	        if not categories:
140	            recent = (
141	                UserPaper.query
142	                .filter_by(user_id=user.id)
143	                .order_by(UserPaper.saved_at.desc())
144	                .limit(5)
145	                .all()
146	            )
147	            for up in recent:
148	                if up.paper.categories:
149	                    categories.extend(up.paper.categories.split())
150	            categories = list(set(categories))
151	
152	        if not categories:
153	            return []
154	
155	        cat = random.choice(categories)
156	        papers = []
157	        try:
158	            batch = ArxivService.trending(
159	                category=cat,
160	                days=7,
161	                max_results=15,
162	                chromadb_service=chromadb_service,
163	            )
164	            for p in batch:
165	                if p.arxiv_id not in seen:
166	                    seen.add(p.arxiv_id)
167	                    papers.append(p)
168	                    if len(papers) >= cls.CATEGORY_COUNT:
169	                        break
170	        except Exception as e:
171	            logger.warning('Category trending fetch failed for %s: %s', cat, e)
172	
173	        return papers
174	
175	    @staticmethod
176	    def _get_saved_arxiv_ids(user_id):
177	        """Return a set of arxiv_ids for papers saved by the user."""
178	        rows = (
179	            db.session.query(Paper.arxiv_id)
180	            .join(UserPaper, UserPaper.paper_id == Paper.id)
181	            .filter(UserPaper.user_id == user_id)
182	            .all()
183	        )
184	        return {r[0] for r in rows}
185	
186	    @staticmethod
187	    def discover_random(category, days=7, count=5, chromadb_service=None):
188	        """Return a random subset of recent papers in a category."""
189	        papers = ArxivService.trending(
190	            category=category,
191	            days=days,
192	            max_results=max(count * 4, 20),
193	            chromadb_service=chromadb_service,
194	        )
195	        if len(papers) <= count:
196	            return papers
197	        return random.sample(papers, count)
198

42	@mcp.tool()
43	def search_papers(query: str, category: str = None, days: int = 30) -> str:
44	    """Search arXiv for papers by keyword and optional category.
45	
46	    Args:
47	        query: Search keywords (e.g. "vision transformer").
48	        category: arXiv category filter (e.g. "cs.CV"). Optional.
49	        days: Only return papers from the last N days. Default 30.
50	    """
51	    with _get_app().app_context():
52	        date_from = (date.today() - timedelta(days=days)).isoformat()
53	        date_to = date.today().isoformat()
54	        papers = ArxivService.search(
55	            query=query,
56	            category=category,
57	            date_from=date_from,
58	            date_to=date_to,
59	            max_results=10,
60	            chromadb_service=_chromadb(),
61	        )
62	        results = [p.to_dict() for p in papers]
63	        return json.dumps(results, indent=2)

85	@mcp.tool()
86	def save_paper(arxiv_id: str, memo: str = None) -> str:
87	    """Save a paper to the user's personal library.
88	
89	    Args:
90	        arxiv_id: The arXiv paper ID (e.g. "2401.12345").
91	        memo: Optional personal note about why you're saving this paper.
92	    """
93	    with _get_app().app_context():
94	        paper = ArxivService.fetch_by_id(arxiv_id, chromadb_service=_chromadb())
95	        if not paper:
96	            return json.dumps({'error': f'Paper {arxiv_id} not found on arXiv.'})
97	
98	        existing = UserPaper.query.filter_by(user_id=_user_id, paper_id=paper.id).first()
99	        if existing:
100	            return json.dumps({'message': 'Paper already saved.', 'arxiv_id': arxiv_id})
101	
102	        up = UserPaper(user_id=_user_id, paper_id=paper.id, memo=memo)
103	        db.session.add(up)
104	        db.session.commit()
105	        return json.dumps({'message': 'Paper saved.', 'arxiv_id': arxiv_id, 'title': paper.title})

173	@mcp.tool()
174	def search_notes(query: str) -> str:
175	    """Semantic search across your personal research notes.
176	
177	    Args:
178	        query: Natural language search query.
179	    """
180	    with _get_app().app_context():
181	        service = _chromadb()
182	        if not service:
183	            return json.dumps([])
184	
185	        try:
186	            results = service.search_notes(query, user_id=_user_id, n_results=5)
187	        except Exception:
188	            return json.dumps([])
189	
190	        items = []
191	        if results and results.get('ids') and results['ids'][0]:
192	            for doc_id, distance in zip(results['ids'][0], results['distances'][0]):
193	                try:
194	                    note_id = int(doc_id.replace('note_', ''))
195	                    note = db.session.get(Note, note_id)
196	                    if note:
197	                        items.append({
198	                            'id': note.id,
199	                            'preview': note.content[:100],
200	                            'arxiv_id': note.paper.arxiv_id if note.paper else None,
201	                            'relevance_score': round(max(0, 1 - distance), 4),
202	                        })
203	                except (ValueError, AttributeError):
204	                    continue
205	        return json.dumps(items, indent=2)

208	@mcp.tool()
209	def search_knowledge(query: str) -> str:
210	    """Search across both papers and personal notes for relevant knowledge.
211	
212	    Args:
213	        query: Natural language search query.
214	    """
215	    with _get_app().app_context():
216	        service = _chromadb()
217	        if not service:
218	            return json.dumps([])
219	
220	        try:
221	            combined = service.search_all(query, user_id=_user_id, n_results=5)
222	        except Exception:
223	            return json.dumps([])
224	
225	        items = []
226	        # Process papers
227	        paper_results = combined.get('papers')
228	        if paper_results and paper_results.get('ids') and paper_results['ids'][0]:
229	            for doc_id, distance, meta in zip(
230	                paper_results['ids'][0],
231	                paper_results['distances'][0],
232	                paper_results['metadatas'][0],
233	            ):
234	                items.append({
235	                    'type': 'paper',
236	                    'arxiv_id': meta.get('arxiv_id', ''),
237	                    'title': meta.get('title', ''),
238	                    'relevance_score': round(max(0, 1 - distance), 4),
239	                })
240	
241	        # Process notes
242	        note_results = combined.get('notes')
243	        if note_results and note_results.get('ids') and note_results['ids'][0]:
244	            for doc_id, distance in zip(note_results['ids'][0], note_results['distances'][0]):
245	                try:
246	                    note_id = int(doc_id.replace('note_', ''))
247	                    note = db.session.get(Note, note_id)
248	                    if note:
249	                        items.append({
250	                            'type': 'note',
251	                            'id': note.id,
252	                            'preview': note.content[:100],
253	                            'arxiv_id': note.paper.arxiv_id if note.paper else None,
254	                            'relevance_score': round(max(0, 1 - distance), 4),
255	                        })
256	                except (ValueError, AttributeError):
257	                    continue
258	
259	        items.sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)
260	        return json.dumps(items, indent=2)

mcp_server.py — Added contextual hints for 5 scenarios:




| Scenario | Tool | Hint |


|----------|------|------|


| No preferred categories | getdailyrecommendations | Tells agent to ask user for categories and update profile |


| Cold start (has categories) | getdailyrecommendations | Suggests saving papers to unlock similarity-based recs |


| Warm start with <5 papers | getdailyrecommendations | Encourages saving more diverse papers |


| Empty results | getdailyrecommendations | Suggests discover_papers with broader params |


| Fewer results than requested | discover_papers | Explains limited arXiv coverage, suggests increasing days |




Hints appear as a hint field in the JSON response only when relevant — no hint is added when everything works normally with sufficient data.

好。然后，对于我想要测试从零开始新建用户的情况，在api侧和mcp侧分别要怎么做？不要进行直接修改，告诉我需要进行的操作即可


Claudeclaude-opus-4-62026-04-14 20:08:55


Claudeclaude-opus-4-62026-04-14 20:09:07
API 侧（HTTP）




    

  1. 注册
    2. 



   ```bash


   curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/register \


     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \


     -d '{"username": "testuser", "email": "test@example.com", "password": "securepass123"}'


   ```




    

  1. 登录，拿 token
    2. 



   ```bash


   curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/login \


     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \


     -d '{"username": "testuser", "password": "securepass123"}'


   ```




    

  1. 设置偏好分类
    2. 



   ```bash


   curl -X PUT http://localhost:5000/api/users/me \


     -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \


     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \


     -d '{"preferred_categories": ["cs.AI"]}'


   ```




    

  1. 获取推荐 / 搜索 / 保存论文 / 写笔记 — 带上 token 正常调用各端点即可
    2. 





MCP 侧




MCP server 通过 --user-id 绑定用户，绕过 JWT，直接读数据库。所以：




    

  1. 先用 API 注册一个用户（MCP 没有注册工具），记下返回的 user_id
    2. 

  2. 重启 MCP server，指定新用户：
    3. 



   ```bash


   python mcp_server.py --user-id <新用户的id>


   ```


   如果是 .mcp.json 配置的，改 args 里的 user-id 后重启 Claude Code


    

  1. 设置偏好分类 — MCP 目前没有 update_profile 工具，有两个选择：
    2. 



   - 通过 API 调用 PUT /api/users/me 设置（需要先登录拿 token）


   - 或者给 MCP 加一个 update_profile 工具




    

  1. 之后就可以直接用 MCP 工具测试完整流程：getdailyrecommendations → 触发 cold start hint → searchpapers / discoverpapers → savepaper → 再次 getdaily_recommendations 观察策略变化
    2. 





核心区别：API 侧自带注册和 profile 更新；MCP 侧缺少这两个能力，需要借助 API 完成用户创建和偏好设置，或者给 MCP 补一个 update_profile 工具。


User2026-04-14 20:11:58
如果考虑mcp独立使用的情景，肯定还是需要能进行注册和用户信息编辑的，这个具体要怎么做呢


Claudeclaude-opus-4-62026-04-14 20:12:10





MCP server 目前已有 Flask app context 和数据库访问，加两个工具即可：




register_user(username, email, password)


    

  • 在 getapp().appcontext() 内直接创建 User 记录（密码用 werkzeug.security.generatepassword_hash 哈希）
    • 

  • 检查 username/email 唯一性，重复则返回错误
    • 

  • 创建成功后自动将 userid 切换为新用户的 id
    • 

  • 返回 {user_id, username, message}
    • 





updateprofile(preferredcategories, email)


    

  • 读取当前 userid 对应的 User，更新传入的字段
    • 

  • preferred_categories 接收逗号分隔的字符串（如 "cs.AI,cs.CV"），转成 list 存入 JSON 字段
    • 

  • 返回更新后的 profile 信息
    • 





两个工具都放在 mcp_server.py 里，和现有工具同级，逻辑很薄——本质就是对 User model 的直接读写，不需要改 service 层或 route 层。

17	def _note_response(note):
18	    """Build a single note response dict with HATEOAS links."""
19	    data = note.to_dict()
20	    data['paper_title'] = note.paper.title
21	    links = {
22	        'self': f'/api/notes/{note.id}',
23	        'paper': f'/api/papers/{note.paper.arxiv_id}',
24	    }
25	    data['_links'] = links
26	    return data

29	def _sync_note_to_chromadb(note, delete=False):
30	    """Sync note content to ChromaDB."""
31	    service = _chromadb()
32	    if not service:
33	        return
34	    try:
35	        if delete:
36	            service.delete_note(note.id)
37	        else:
38	            service.add_note(
39	                note_id=note.id,
40	                content=note.content,
41	                metadata={
42	                    'user_id': note.user_id,
43	                    'paper_id': note.paper.arxiv_id,
44	                    'created_at': note.created_at.isoformat(),
45	                },
46	            )
47	    except Exception:
48	        pass  # non-critical
49

51	def _validate_content(content):
52	    """Validate note content length."""
53	    if len(content) > NOTE_MAX_LENGTH:
54	        raise APIError(
55	            f'Content exceeds maximum length of {NOTE_MAX_LENGTH} characters.',
56	            400,
57	        )

60	@notes_bp.route('/notes', methods=['POST'])
61	@jwt_required()
62	def create_note():
63	    """Create a new insight note linked to a paper.
64	    ---
65	    tags:
66	      - Notes
67	    security:
68	      - Bearer: []
69	    parameters:
70	      - in: body
71	        name: body
72	        required: true
73	        schema:
74	          type: object
75	          required:
76	            - paper_id
77	            - content
78	          properties:
79	            paper_id:
80	              type: string
81	              description: arXiv ID to link the note to (required)
82	              example: "2301.07041"
83	            content:
84	              type: string
85	              description: Insight content (max 1000 characters)
86	              example: The paper shows multi-head attention can be pruned without significant performance loss.
87	    responses:
88	      201:
89	        description: Note created successfully
90	      400:
91	        description: Missing required fields or content too long
92	      404:
93	        description: Linked paper not found
94	    """
95	    uid = int(get_jwt_identity())
96	    data = request.get_json(silent=True)
97	    validate_required_fields(data, ['paper_id', 'content'])
98	    _validate_content(data['content'])
99	
100	    arxiv_id = data['paper_id']
101	    paper = Paper.query.filter_by(arxiv_id=arxiv_id).first()
102	    if not paper:
103	        raise APIError(f"Paper with arxiv_id '{arxiv_id}' not found.", 404)
104	
105	    note = Note(
106	        user_id=uid,
107	        paper_id=paper.id,
108	        content=data['content'],
109	    )
110	    db.session.add(note)
111	    db.session.commit()
112	
113	    _sync_note_to_chromadb(note)
114	
115	    return jsonify({
116	        'data': _note_response(note),
117	    }), 201

120	@notes_bp.route('/notes', methods=['GET'])
121	@jwt_required()
122	def list_notes():
123	    """List all notes for the authenticated user.
124	    ---
125	    tags:
126	      - Notes
127	    security:
128	      - Bearer: []
129	    parameters:
130	      - in: query
131	        name: paper_id
132	        type: string
133	        required: false
134	        description: Filter by arXiv paper ID
135	        example: "2301.07041"
136	      - in: query
137	        name: page
138	        type: integer
139	        required: false
140	        default: 1
141	        description: Page number
142	      - in: query
143	        name: per_page
144	        type: integer
145	        required: false
146	        default: 20
147	        description: Results per page (max 100)
148	    responses:
149	      200:
150	        description: Paginated list of notes
151	    """
152	    uid = int(get_jwt_identity())
153	    page = request.args.get('page', 1, type=int)
154	    per_page = request.args.get('per_page', 20, type=int)
155	    per_page = min(per_page, 100)
156	
157	    query = Note.query.filter_by(user_id=uid)
158	
159	    # Optional filter by paper arxiv_id
160	    paper_id_filter = request.args.get('paper_id')
161	    if paper_id_filter:
162	        paper = Paper.query.filter_by(arxiv_id=paper_id_filter).first()
163	        if paper:
164	            query = query.filter_by(paper_id=paper.id)
165	        else:
166	            query = query.filter(False)
167	
168	    query = query.order_by(Note.updated_at.desc())
169	    pagination = query.paginate(page=page, per_page=per_page, error_out=False)
170	
171	    data = [_note_response(n) for n in pagination.items]
172	    pages = pagination.pages or 1
173	
174	    return jsonify({
175	        'data': data,
176	        'pagination': {
177	            'total': pagination.total,
178	            'page': page,
179	            'per_page': per_page,
180	            'pages': pages,
181	        },
182	        '_links': {
183	            'self': f'/api/notes?page={page}&per_page={per_page}',
184	            **(
185	                {'next': f'/api/notes?page={page+1}&per_page={per_page}'}
186	                if pagination.has_next else {}
187	            ),
188	            **(
189	                {'prev': f'/api/notes?page={page-1}&per_page={per_page}'}
190	                if pagination.has_prev else {}
191	            ),
192	        },
193	    }), 200

12	def _chromadb():
13	    """Get the ChromaDB service from app extensions."""
14	    return current_app.extensions.get('chromadb')

17	def _clamp(value, lo=0.0, hi=1.0):
18	    """Clamp a numeric value to [lo, hi]."""
19	    return max(lo, min(hi, value))
20	
21	
22	def _build_paper_result(paper, distance):
23	    """Build a single paper search result dict."""
24	    relevance_score = round(_clamp(1.0 - distance), 4)
25	    return {
26	        'arxiv_id': paper.arxiv_id,
27	        'title': paper.title,
28	        'abstract': paper.abstract,
29	        'categories': paper.categories,
30	        'published_date': paper.published_date.isoformat(),
31	        'relevance_score': relevance_score,
32	        'type': 'paper',
33	        '_links': {
34	            'self': f'/api/papers/{paper.arxiv_id}',
35	            'save': f'/api/papers/{paper.arxiv_id}/save',
36	        },
37	    }
38	
39	
40	def _build_note_result(note, distance):
41	    """Build a single note search result dict."""
42	    relevance_score = round(_clamp(1.0 - distance), 4)
43	    return {
44	        'id': note.id,
45	        'preview': note.content[:100] + ('...' if len(note.content) > 100 else ''),
46	        'content': note.content,
47	        'arxiv_id': note.paper.arxiv_id,
48	        'relevance_score': relevance_score,
49	        'type': 'note',
50	        '_links': {
51	            'self': f'/api/notes/{note.id}',
52	            'paper': f'/api/papers/{note.paper.arxiv_id}',
53	        },
54	    }
55	
56	
57	def _parse_search_body(default_n=10):
58	    """Parse and validate the search request body."""
59	    data = request.get_json(silent=True)
60	    if not data or not data.get('query'):
61	        raise APIError('Field "query" is required.', 400)
62	    query = data['query'].strip()
63	    if not query:
64	        raise APIError('Field "query" must not be empty.', 400)
65	    n_results = data.get('n_results', default_n)
66	    if not isinstance(n_results, int) or n_results < 1:
67	        raise APIError('"n_results" must be a positive integer.', 400)
68	    n_results = min(n_results, 50)
69	    return query, n_results
70	
71	
72	def _process_paper_results(results):
73	    """Convert ChromaDB paper results into response dicts."""
74	    items = []
75	    if not results or not results.get('ids') or not results['ids'][0]:
76	        return items
77	
78	    ids = results['ids'][0]
79	    distances = results['distances'][0]
80	    metadatas = results['metadatas'][0]
81	
82	    for doc_id, distance, metadata in zip(ids, distances, metadatas):
83	        arxiv_id = metadata.get('arxiv_id', '')
84	        if not arxiv_id:
85	            # Fallback: strip "paper_" prefix from the ChromaDB document ID
86	            arxiv_id = doc_id.replace('paper_', '', 1) if doc_id.startswith('paper_') else doc_id
87	
88	        paper = Paper.query.filter_by(arxiv_id=arxiv_id).first()
89	        if not paper:
90	            continue
91	
92	        items.append(_build_paper_result(paper, distance))
93	    return items
94	
95	
96	def _process_note_results(results):
97	    """Convert ChromaDB note results into response dicts."""
98	    items = []
99	    if not results or not results.get('ids') or not results['ids'][0]:
100	        return items
101	
102	    ids = results['ids'][0]
103	    distances = results['distances'][0]
104	
105	    for doc_id, distance in zip(ids, distances):
106	        # ChromaDB note IDs are formatted as "note_{id}"
107	        try:
108	            note_id = int(doc_id.replace('note_', '', 1))
109	        except (ValueError, AttributeError):
110	            continue
111	
112	        note = db.session.get(Note, note_id)
113	        if not note:
114	            continue
115	
116	        items.append(_build_note_result(note, distance))
117	    return items
118
