120	@search_bp.route('/search/papers', methods=['POST'])
121	def search_papers():
122	    """Semantic search over paper abstracts using ChromaDB.
123	    ---
124	    tags:
125	      - Semantic Search
126	    parameters:
127	      - in: body
128	        name: body
129	        required: true
130	        schema:
131	          type: object
132	          required:
133	            - query
134	          properties:
135	            query:
136	              type: string
137	              example: "transformer attention mechanism"
138	            n_results:
139	              type: integer
140	              default: 10
141	              description: Number of results to return (max 50)
142	    responses:
143	      200:
144	        description: Semantic search results from paper abstracts
145	        schema:
146	          type: object
147	          properties:
148	            data:
149	              type: array
150	              items:
151	                type: object
152	                properties:
153	                  arxiv_id:
154	                    type: string
155	                  title:
156	                    type: string
157	                  abstract:
158	                    type: string
159	                  relevance_score:
160	                    type: number
161	                    description: "Similarity score 0-1 (higher = more relevant)"
162	                  type:
163	                    type: string
164	                    example: paper
165	            query:
166	              type: string
167	            source:
168	              type: string
169	              example: paper_abstracts
170	      400:
171	        description: Missing or empty query field
172	    """
173	    query, n_results = _parse_search_body(default_n=10)
174	
175	    service = _chromadb()
176	    if not service:
177	        return jsonify({'data': [], 'query': query, 'source': 'paper_abstracts'}), 200
178	
179	    try:
180	        results = service.search_papers(query, n_results=n_results)
181	    except Exception:
182	        return jsonify({'data': [], 'query': query, 'source': 'paper_abstracts'}), 200
183	
184	    items = _process_paper_results(results)
185	
186	    return jsonify({
187	        'data': items,
188	        'query': query,
189	        'source': 'paper_abstracts',
190	    }), 200

229	                  id:
230	                    type: integer
231	                  title:
232	                    type: string
233	                  content:
234	                    type: string
235	                  relevance_score:
236	                    type: number
237	                  type:
238	                    type: string
239	                    example: note
240	            query:
241	              type: string
242	            source:
243	              type: string
244	              example: user_notes
245	      400:
246	        description: Missing or empty query field
247	      401:
248	        description: Missing or invalid JWT token
249	    """
250	    uid = int(get_jwt_identity())
251	    query, n_results = _parse_search_body(default_n=5)
252	
253	    service = _chromadb()
254	    if not service:
255	        return jsonify({'data': [], 'query': query, 'source': 'user_notes'}), 200
256	
257	    try:
258	        results = service.search_notes(query, user_id=uid, n_results=n_results)
259	    except Exception:
260	        return jsonify({'data': [], 'query': query, 'source': 'user_notes'}), 200
261	
262	    items = _process_note_results(results)
263	
264	    return jsonify({
265	        'data': items,
266	        'query': query,
267	        'source': 'user_notes',
268	    }), 200
269	
270	
271	@search_bp.route('/search/all', methods=['POST'])
272	@jwt_required()
273	def search_all():
274	    """Search across both papers and notes, merged by relevance.
275	    ---
276	    tags:
277	      - Semantic Search
278	    security:
279	      - Bearer: []
280	    parameters:
281	      - in: body
282	        name: body
283	        required: true
284	        schema:
285	          type: object
286	          required:
287	            - query
288	          properties:
289	            query:
290	              type: string
291	              example: "attention mechanism improvements"
292	            n_results:
293	              type: integer
294	              default: 10
295	              description: Number of results per source (max 50)
296	    responses:
297	      200:
298	        description: Combined results from papers and notes sorted by relevance
299	        schema:
300	          type: object
301	          properties:
302	            data:
303	              type: array
304	              items:
305	                type: object
306	                properties:
307	                  type:
308	                    type: string
309	                    enum: [paper, note]
310	                  relevance_score:
311	                    type: number
312	            query:
313	              type: string
314	            source:
315	              type: string
316	              example: all
317	      400:
318	        description: Missing or empty query field
319	      401:
320	        description: Missing or invalid JWT token
321	    """
322	    uid = int(get_jwt_identity())
323	    query, n_results = _parse_search_body(default_n=10)
324	
325	    service = _chromadb()
326	    if not service:
327	        return jsonify({'data': [], 'query': query, 'source': 'all'}), 200
328	
329	    try:
330	        combined = service.search_all(query, user_id=uid, n_results=n_results)
331	    except Exception:
332	        return jsonify({'data': [], 'query': query, 'source': 'all'}), 200
333	
334	    paper_items = _process_paper_results(combined.get('papers'))
335	    note_items = _process_note_results(combined.get('notes'))
336	
337	    merged = paper_items + note_items
338	    merged.sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)
339	
340	    return jsonify({
341	        'data': merged,
342	        'query': query,
343	        'source': 'all',
344	    }), 200
345

1	# ScholarTrack
2	
3	A RESTful Web API for researchers to discover and track arXiv papers, record insights, and get personalized recommendations. Built with Flask for the XJCO3011 Web Services and Web Data coursework.
4	
5	## Features
6	
7	- **Authentication (F1)** — Register, login, JWT-based access control
8	- **Paper Discovery (F2)** — Search arXiv, browse trending papers, random discovery
9	- **Paper Management (F3)** — Save papers to a personal library with tags and memos
10	- **Insight Notes (F4)** — Short annotations linked to papers (max 1000 chars)
11	- **Recommendations (F5)** — Personalized daily paper recommendations (cold/warm start)
12	- **RAG Semantic Search (F6)** — Vector search over paper abstracts and notes via ChromaDB
13	- **MCP Server (F7)** — AI assistant integration through the Model Context Protocol
14	
15	## Tech Stack
16	
17	| Component | Technology |
18	|-----------|-----------|
19	| Framework | Flask 3.1.1 |
20	| Database | SQLite + SQLAlchemy 2.0 |
21	| Authentication | JWT (flask-jwt-extended) |
22	| Vector Search | ChromaDB 1.0.7 |
23	| External API | arXiv Python client |
24	| API Documentation | Flasgger (Swagger/OpenAPI) |
25	| Testing | pytest + pytest-cov |
26	
27	## Quick Start
28	
29	### Prerequisites
30	
31	- Python 3.11+
32	- Conda (recommended)
33	
34	### Installation
35	
36	```bash
37	# Clone the repository
38	git clone https://github.com/Nuo-cl/ScholarTrack.git
39	cd ScholarTrack
40	
41	# Create conda environment
42	conda create -n scholartrack python=3.11
43	conda activate scholartrack
44	
45	# Install dependencies
46	pip install -r requirements.txt
47	```
48	
49	### Running the Server
50	
51	```bash
52	python run.py
53	```
54	
55	The API server starts at `http://localhost:5000`. Swagger UI is available at `http://localhost:5000/apidocs`.
56	
57	### Running Tests
58	
59	```bash
60	pytest                        # Run all tests
61	pytest --cov=app tests/       # Run with coverage report
62	pytest tests/test_auth.py -v  # Run a specific test module
63	```
64	
65	## MCP Server
66	
67	ScholarTrack includes an MCP (Model Context Protocol) server that exposes core functionality as tools for AI assistants such as Claude. The MCP server calls the service layer directly (not via HTTP), so the Flask web server does not need to be running.
68	
69	### Available Tools
70	
71	| Tool | Description |
72	|------|-------------|
73	| `search_papers` | Search arXiv by keyword, category, and time range |
74	| `get_trending_papers` | Get recent trending papers in an arXiv category |
75	| `get_daily_recommendations` | Personalized daily paper recommendations |
76	| `discover_papers` | Random paper discovery for serendipitous browsing |
77	| `save_paper` | Save a paper to the user's library |
78	| `list_library` | List all saved papers |
79	| `create_note` | Record a short insight note linked to a paper |
80	| `search_notes` | Semantic search across personal notes |
81	| `search_knowledge` | Search across both papers and notes |
82	
83	### Running Standalone
84	
85	```bash
86	python mcp_server.py [--user-id USER_ID]
87	```
88	
89	The `--user-id` flag specifies which user's data to operate on (default: 1). The MCP server bypasses JWT authentication and accesses the database directly.
90	
91	### Configuring with Claude Code
92	
93	Create a `.mcp.json` file in the project root:
94	
95	```json
96	{
97	  "mcpServers": {
98	    "scholartrack": {
99	      "command": "python",
100	      "args": ["mcp_server.py", "--user-id", "1"],
101	      "cwd": "/path/to/ScholarTrack"
102	    }
103	  }
104	}
105	```
106	
107	After restarting Claude Code, the AI assistant can directly invoke tools like `search_papers`, `get_daily_recommendations`, etc.
108	
109	### Configuring with Claude Desktop
110	
111	Add the following to your Claude Desktop MCP settings (`claude_desktop_config.json`):
112	
113	```json
114	{
115	  "mcpServers": {
116	    "scholartrack": {
117	      "command": "python",
118	      "args": ["mcp_server.py", "--user-id", "1"],
119	      "cwd": "/path/to/ScholarTrack"
120	    }
121	  }
122	}
123	```
124	
125	## REST API
126	
127	All endpoints are under the `/api` prefix. Authenticated endpoints require a JWT bearer token:
128	
129	```
130	Authorization: Bearer <access_token>
131	```
132	
133	### Endpoint Summary
134	
135	| Module | Key Endpoints | Auth |
136	|--------|--------------|------|
137	| Authentication (F1) | `POST /auth/register`, `POST /auth/login`, `GET /users/me`, `PUT /users/me` | Partial |
138	| Paper Discovery (F2) | `GET /papers/search`, `GET /papers/trending`, `GET /papers/discover`, `GET /papers/<id>` | No |
139	| Paper Management (F3) | `POST /papers/<id>/save`, `GET /library`, `POST /library/<id>/tags` | Yes |
140	| Notes (F4) | `POST /notes`, `GET /notes`, `GET /papers/<id>/notes`, `PUT /notes/<id>` | Yes |
141	| Recommendations (F5) | `GET /recommendations/daily` | Yes |
142	| Semantic Search (F6) | `POST /search/papers`, `POST /search/notes`, `POST /search/all` | Partial |
143	
144	Interactive Swagger UI with full request/response examples is at `/apidocs` when the server is running. Detailed API documentation is available in [`docs/api_documentation.pdf`](docs/api_documentation.pdf).
145	
146	### Quick Example
147	
148	```bash
149	# Register and login
150	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/register \
151	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
152	  -d '{"username": "researcher1", "email": "r1@example.com", "password": "securepass123"}'
153	
154	curl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/login \
155	  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
156	  -d '{"username": "researcher1", "password": "securepass123"}'
157	# -> returns { "data": { "access_token": "eyJ..." } }
158	
159	# Search papers (no auth required)
160	curl "http://localhost:5000/api/papers/search?q=vision+transformer&category=cs.CV"
161	
162	# Get daily recommendations (auth required)
163	curl http://localhost:5000/api/recommendations/daily \
164	  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>"
165	```
166	
167	## Project Structure
168	
169	```
170	app/
171	├── __init__.py          # Flask app factory
172	├── config.py            # Configuration (dev/test/prod)
173	├── models/              # SQLAlchemy models (6 tables)
174	├── routes/              # API endpoints (5 Blueprint modules)
175	├── services/            # Business logic (arXiv, ChromaDB, recommendations)
176	└── utils/               # Error handling, pagination, validation
177	tests/                   # pytest test suite
178	docs/                    # Design specs and API documentation
179	mcp_server.py            # MCP server for AI assistants
180	```
181

183	
184	This project is coursework for XJCO3011 at the University of Leeds.

这个文件包含所有消息的原始 JSON 记录，包括被压缩掉的部分。你可以：
